  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:right;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;">	</font><img src="img52906712_0.jpg" alt="img52906712_0.jpg" style="width:162px;height:62px;"></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Terns Pharmaceuticals Reports First Quarter 2023 Financial Results and Corporate Updates</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">- Top-line data from Phase 2a DUET clinical trial of TERN-501 (THR-&#x3b2; agonist) in NASH expected in third quarter of 2023</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">- TERN-701 (allosteric BCR-ABL) Phase 1 trial for CML on track to initiate in the U.S. in second half of 2023; enrollment progress update from ongoing China Phase 1 trial expected at the 2023 ASCO Annual Meeting</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">-  TERN-601 (GLP-1) program in obesity on track to initiate Phase 1 clinical trial in second half of 2023 with initial proof of concept data anticipated in 2024</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">- Cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities of $298 million expected to provide runway into 2026</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">FOSTER CITY, Calif., May 15, 2023 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) &#x2013; Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. (&#x201c;Terns&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;) (Nasdaq: TERN), a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a portfolio of small-molecule product candidates to address serious diseases, including oncology, non-alcoholic steatohepatitis (NASH) and obesity, today reported financial results for the first quarter ended March 31, 2023 and corporate updates.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;We are excited to announce plans to share key clinical and preclinical updates across our three lead programs at upcoming scientific congresses and look forward to several important clinical milestones later this year,&#x201d; said Sen Sundaram, chief executive officer at Terns. &#x201c;We anticipate top-line data from our Phase 2a DUET trial of TERN-501 as a treatment for NASH in the third quarter and the initiation of Phase 1 clinical trials in our chronic myeloid leukemia (CML) and obesity programs in the second half of this year. In addition, I&#x2019;m impressed with the progress our partner, Hansoh, has made in enrolling the Phase 1 trial in China so quickly and hope we will see early data accepted for presentation by the end of the year. We continue to rapidly advance our development programs with the goal of making a significant difference in the lives of people living with serious diseases.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Recent Developments and Anticipated Milestones</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">TERN-701: Oral, allosteric BCR-ABL tyrosine kinase inhibitor (TKI) for chronic myeloid leukemia (CML)</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Terns expects to initiate a clinical trial for TERN-701 in the United States in the second half of 2023, with potential top-line readouts from initial dose-escalation cohorts in 2024</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.065%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.989278055754109%;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Phase 1 trial for TERN-701 is expected to include sites from U.S., Europe and other countries</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">A poster detailing non-clinical xenograft activity of TERN-701 will be presented at the American Society for Pharmacology and Experimental Therapeutics (ASPET) on May 18, 2023 at 5:00 PM CDT</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">A trial-in-progress (TiP) poster and status update will be presented at the 2023 ASCO Annual Meeting on June 5, 2023 at 8:00 AM CDT summarizing the ongoing Phase 1 study of TERN-701 (HS-10382) in China </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.065%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.989278055754109%;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Phase 1 trial is a dose-escalation and dose-expansion trial (</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NCT05367700</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">) evaluating the tolerability, efficacy, and pharmacokinetics of once-daily TERN-701 (HS-10382) in approximately 100 people with CML in China conducted by Terns&#x2019; partner Hansoh Pharmaceutical Group</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Terns welcomed Emil Kuriakose, M.D. as Chief Medical Officer of Terns Oncology in May 2023. Dr. Kuriakose brings more than a decade of oncology clinical development and medical affairs experience</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Terns plans to host a virtual R&amp;D event with a focus on the evolving CML treatment paradigm and the potential role for TERN-701 in July 2023</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:7.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">TERN-501: Oral, thyroid hormone receptor-beta (THR-&#x3b2;) agonist for NASH</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Phase 2a DUET trial (</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NCT05415722</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">), evaluating TERN-501 as a monotherapy and in combination with TERN-101 (farnesoid X receptor (FXR) agonist), completed enrollment in February 2023 with top-line data expected in the third quarter of 2023</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.065%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.989278055754109%;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Primary endpoint is the relative change from baseline in liver fat content as measured by MRI protein density fat fraction (MRI-PDFF) at Week 12 for TERN-501 monotherapy compared with placebo</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.065%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.989278055754109%;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Secondary endpoints include assessment of safety and tolerability, pharmacokinetics, changes in MRI-PDFF and MRI corrected T1 (cT1)</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.065%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.989278055754109%;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">DUET is the first clinical trial assessing a THR-&#x3b2; agonist as monotherapy and in combination with an FXR agonist in people with NASH</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">TERN-601: Oral, small-molecule glucagon-like peptide-1 (GLP-1) receptor agonist for obesity</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Terns&#x2019; lead GLP-1 receptor agonist program remains on track to initiate a Phase 1 first-in-human clinical trial in subjects with elevated BMI in the second half of 2023, with top-line data expected in 2024</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">A poster evaluating activity of TERN-601 in transgenic mice expressing human GLP-1 receptor will be presented at a major diabetes conference in June 2023</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">TERN-800: Oral, small-molecule glucose-dependent insulinotropic polypeptide receptor (GIPR) modulators for obesity</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Lead structural series of GIPR modulators have been identified, with lead optimization efforts underway </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Candidate nomination and initiation of IND-enabling activities expected in 2024</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">GIPR modulators have the potential for combination with GLP-1 receptor agonists, such as TERN-601</font></div></div>

  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Research and Development (R&amp;D) Expenses: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">R&amp;D expenses were $17.1 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2023, as compared with $8.1 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2022.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">General and Administrative (G&amp;A) Expenses:</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> G&amp;A expenses were $7.1 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2023, as compared with $5.7 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2022.</font></div></div>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About Terns Pharmaceuticals</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a portfolio of small-molecule product candidates to address serious diseases, including oncology, NASH and obesity. Terns&#x2019; pipeline includes two clinical stage development programs including an allosteric BCR-ABL inhibitor and a THR-&#x3b2; agonist (+/- an FXR agonist), and preclinical small-molecule GLP-1 receptor agonist and GIPR modulator programs. For more information, please visit: www.ternspharma.com.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
